{
  "title": "USER STORY: Compare Product Performance",
  "body": "### Epic 6: Sales and Analytics\r\n\r\n*As an admin, I can compare the performance of multiple products side by side so that I can make informed inventory or marketing decisions.*\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Acceptance Criteria**\r\n\r\n- Admins can view a dashboard comparing product performance metrics such as sales volume, revenue generated, and customer ratings.\r\n- The comparison includes key metrics like total units sold, total revenue, average customer rating, and total page views.\r\n- The dashboard allows filtering by product categories and specific date ranges.\r\n- Data is displayed in a table format with optional graphical visualisations (e.g., bar charts, line graphs).\r\n- Admins can export the comparison data as a CSV file for further analysis.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Tasks**\r\n\r\n**Dashboard Design**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Design a product comparison dashboard in the admin interface.\r\n- [ ] Include a table to display metrics like total units sold, revenue, average rating, and page views for selected products.\r\n\r\n**Data Filtering**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Implement filters to narrow the data by product categories and date ranges.\r\n- [ ] Add a multi-select dropdown for choosing specific products to compare.\r\n\r\n**Graphical Visualisations**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Create bar charts or line graphs to visualise product sales and revenue trends side by side.\r\n- [ ] Add toggle options to switch between tabular and graphical views.\r\n\r\n**Export Functionality**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Implement a button to export the comparison data as a CSV file.\r\n- [ ] Ensure the exported data includes all selected metrics and filters.\r\n\r\n**Testing**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Verify the dashboard displays accurate product performance data for the selected products.\r\n- [ ] Test the filtering options to ensure they update the displayed data correctly.\r\n- [ ] Validate the graphical visualisations for clarity and usability.\r\n- [ ] Confirm the CSV export functionality works as expected, including applying filters to the exported data.\r\n\r\n---\r\n"
}

  "body": "### Epic 5: Admin Product Management\r\n\r\n*As an admin, I can view a summary of product inventory so that I can monitor stock levels easily.*\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Acceptance Criteria**\r\n\r\n- Admins can view a summary of inventory levels for all products in the admin panel.\r\n- The summary includes product name, SKU, current stock level, and restock status (e.g., low stock, out of stock).\r\n- Products are sorted by stock level in ascending order by default, with low or out-of-stock items prioritised.\r\n- Admins can filter inventory by categories or stock status.\r\n- The summary dynamically updates to reflect recent changes in stock levels.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Tasks**\r\n\r\n**Inventory Summary**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Add an inventory summary section to the admin panel displaying product name, SKU, stock level, and restock status.\r\n- [ ] Highlight low stock and out-of-stock products for easy identification.\r\n\r\n**Sorting and Filtering**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Implement sorting functionality to arrange products by stock level or SKU.\r\n- [ ] Add filters to view inventory by product category or stock status.\r\n\r\n**Dynamic Updates**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Ensure the inventory summary dynamically reflects stock level changes due to sales or restocking.\r\n\r\n**Feedback Messages**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Display notifications (e.g., *\"Inventory updated successfully.\"*) when stock levels are changed manually.\r\n- [ ] Show warnings for critically low stock levels or out-of-stock items.\r\n\r\n**Testing**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Verify the inventory summary displays accurate stock levels for all products.\r\n- [ ] Test sorting and filtering functionality to ensure it works as expected.\r\n- [ ] Validate that the summary updates dynamically when stock levels change.\r\n- [ ] Ensure the interface is responsive and functions correctly across devices and browsers.\r\n\r\n---\r\n"

  "title": "USER STORY: Minimal Load Times",
  "body": "### Epic 1: User Experience (UX)\r\n\r\n*As a user, I can experience minimal load times on every page so that I don't lose interest or abandon the site.*\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Acceptance Criteria**\r\n\r\n- All pages load within 3 seconds under normal internet conditions.\r\n- Images and videos are optimized for quick loading without compromising quality.\r\n- Minified CSS, JavaScript, and HTML are used to reduce file sizes.\r\n- Unused CSS and JavaScript are removed to improve performance.\r\n- Third-party scripts are optimized or loaded asynchronously where possible.\r\n- Browser caching is implemented for static assets.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Tasks**\r\n\r\n**Image and Video Optimization**\r\n\r\n- [x] Compress all images in the */media/* directory using a tool like TinyPNG or ImageOptim.\r\n- [x] Ensure videos (if any) are optimized for web delivery with reduced file sizes.\r\n- [x] Implement responsive image loading using the `srcset` attribute.\r\n\r\n**Minification and Cleanup**\r\n\r\n- [x] Minify all CSS files in */static/css/* and JavaScript files in */static/js/*.\r\n- [x] Remove any unused CSS or JavaScript detected during performance audits.\r\n\r\n**Third-Party Script Optimization**\r\n\r\n- [x] Load third-party scripts asynchronously or defer their loading when possible.\r\n- [x] Evaluate the necessity of third-party libraries and remove any redundant ones.\r\n\r\n**Caching and Headers**\r\n\r\n- [x] Implement browser caching for static files to improve repeat visit load times.\r\n- [x] Add cache-control headers for assets served from the server.\r\n\r\n**Performance Testing**\r\n\r\n- [x] Use tools like Lighthouse or GTmetrix to evaluate page performance.\r\n- [x] Identify and resolve any bottlenecks causing slow load times.\r\n- [x] Test page loading times across different devices and browsers.\r\n\r\n**Monitoring**\r\n\r\n- [x] Regularly review and address any performance degradation.\r\n\r\n---\r\n"
}
{
  "title": "USER STORY: Accessibility Features",
  "body": "### Epic 1: User Experience (UX)\r\n\r\n*As a user with disabilities, I can use assistive technologies (e.g., screen readers) to navigate the site so that I can access the same features as any other user.*\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Acceptance Criteria**\r\n\r\n- All interactive elements (e.g., buttons, links, and forms) are accessible via keyboard navigation.\r\n- ARIA roles and labels are correctly implemented for interactive and navigational elements.\r\n- Text content meets WCAG AA standards for contrast ratios, ensuring readability.\r\n- Images include descriptive alt text for screen readers.\r\n- Toast notifications and error messages are accessible to screen readers.\r\n- The site provides clear focus indicators for active elements.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Tasks**\r\n\r\n**Keyboard Navigation**\r\n\r\n- [x] Test all buttons, links, and forms to ensure they are navigable using the keyboard alone.\r\n- [x] Add focus states to CSS for interactive elements to make active selections visually apparent.\r\n\r\n**ARIA Implementation**\r\n\r\n- [x] Add ARIA roles to navigation menus, buttons, and form elements.\r\n- [x] Use ARIA labels to provide context for elements like *hamburger menus* and icons.\r\n\r\n**Contrast and Readability**\r\n\r\n- [x] Evaluate all text and background color combinations for WCAG AA compliance.\r\n- [x] Adjust styles in *base.css* to improve text readability where necessary.\r\n\r\n**Alt Text for Images**\r\n\r\n- [x] Add descriptive alt text for all images in the */media/* directory and templates.\r\n- [x] Test alt text with a screen reader to ensure it provides useful descriptions.\r\n\r\n**Accessible Notifications**\r\n\r\n- [x] Implement ARIA live regions for dynamic elements like error messages and toasts.\r\n\r\n**Testing**\r\n\r\n- [x] Conduct usability testing with keyboard-only navigation to ensure full functionality.\r\n- [x] Validate that all elements meet WCAG AA standards for accessibility.\r\n"
}

  "body": "### Epic 3: Checkout and Payment\r\n\r\n*As a user, I can see an error message if my payment fails so that I know to retry or use a different method.*\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Acceptance Criteria**\r\n\r\n- An error message is displayed immediately if a payment fails during checkout.\r\n- The error message is clear and specific, indicating the reason for the failure (e.g., *\"Card declined.\"*, *\"Insufficient funds.\"*).\r\n- The error message provides actionable guidance, such as retrying the payment or using a different payment method.\r\n- The checkout process remains open, allowing the user to make corrections or try another payment method.\r\n- The error message is styled consistently with the website's design and is easily noticeable.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Tasks**\r\n\r\n**Error Message Display**\r\n\r\n- [x] Add functionality to display error messages when payment failures occur.\r\n- [x] Ensure the error messages appear near the payment form for visibility.\r\n\r\n**Backend Integration**\r\n\r\n- [x] Implement logic to capture and relay payment failure reasons from the payment gateway (e.g., Stripe).\r\n- [x] Map error codes from the gateway to user-friendly messages.\r\n\r\n**User Feedback**\r\n\r\n- [x] Display actionable suggestions in the error message (e.g., *\"Please check your card details and try again.\"*).\r\n\r\n**Testing**\r\n\r\n- [x] Test payment failure scenarios (e.g., invalid card details, insufficient funds) to ensure error messages display correctly.\r\n- [x] Verify the error messages are clear, actionable, and styled appropriately.\r\n- [x] Ensure the user can retry the payment or choose a different method without restarting the checkout process.\r\n- [x] Validate the functionality across devices and browsers.\r\n\r\n---\r\n"

  "title": "USER STORY: Minimal Load Times",
  "body": "### Epic 1: User Experience (UX)\r\n\r\n*As a user, I can experience minimal load times on every page so that I don't lose interest or abandon the site.*\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Acceptance Criteria**\r\n\r\n- All pages load within 3 seconds under normal internet conditions.\r\n- Images and videos are optimized for quick loading without compromising quality.\r\n- Minified CSS, JavaScript, and HTML are used to reduce file sizes.\r\n- Unused CSS and JavaScript are removed to improve performance.\r\n- Third-party scripts are optimized or loaded asynchronously where possible.\r\n- Browser caching is implemented for static assets.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Tasks**\r\n\r\n**Image and Video Optimization**\r\n\r\n- [x] Compress all images in the */media/* directory using a tool like TinyPNG or ImageOptim.\r\n- [x] Ensure videos (if any) are optimized for web delivery with reduced file sizes.\r\n- [x] Implement responsive image loading using the `srcset` attribute.\r\n\r\n**Minification and Cleanup**\r\n\r\n- [x] Minify all CSS files in */static/css/* and JavaScript files in */static/js/*.\r\n- [x] Remove any unused CSS or JavaScript detected during performance audits.\r\n\r\n**Third-Party Script Optimization**\r\n\r\n- [x] Load third-party scripts asynchronously or defer their loading when possible.\r\n- [x] Evaluate the necessity of third-party libraries and remove any redundant ones.\r\n\r\n**Caching and Headers**\r\n\r\n- [x] Implement browser caching for static files to improve repeat visit load times.\r\n- [x] Add cache-control headers for assets served from the server.\r\n\r\n**Performance Testing**\r\n\r\n- [x] Use tools like Lighthouse or GTmetrix to evaluate page performance.\r\n- [x] Identify and resolve any bottlenecks causing slow load times.\r\n- [x] Test page loading times across different devices and browsers.\r\n\r\n**Monitoring**\r\n\r\n- [x] Regularly review and address any performance degradation.\r\n\r\n---\r\n"
}
{
  "title": "USER STORY: Accessibility Features",
  "body": "### Epic 1: User Experience (UX)\r\n\r\n*As a user with disabilities, I can use assistive technologies (e.g., screen readers) to navigate the site so that I can access the same features as any other user.*\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Acceptance Criteria**\r\n\r\n- All interactive elements (e.g., buttons, links, and forms) are accessible via keyboard navigation.\r\n- ARIA roles and labels are correctly implemented for interactive and navigational elements.\r\n- Text content meets WCAG AA standards for contrast ratios, ensuring readability.\r\n- Images include descriptive alt text for screen readers.\r\n- Toast notifications and error messages are accessible to screen readers.\r\n- The site provides clear focus indicators for active elements.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Tasks**\r\n\r\n**Keyboard Navigation**\r\n\r\n- [x] Test all buttons, links, and forms to ensure they are navigable using the keyboard alone.\r\n- [x] Add focus states to CSS for interactive elements to make active selections visually apparent.\r\n\r\n**ARIA Implementation**\r\n\r\n- [x] Add ARIA roles to navigation menus, buttons, and form elements.\r\n- [x] Use ARIA labels to provide context for elements like *hamburger menus* and icons.\r\n\r\n**Contrast and Readability**\r\n\r\n- [x] Evaluate all text and background color combinations for WCAG AA compliance.\r\n- [x] Adjust styles in *base.css* to improve text readability where necessary.\r\n\r\n**Alt Text for Images**\r\n\r\n- [x] Add descriptive alt text for all images in the */media/* directory and templates.\r\n- [x] Test alt text with a screen reader to ensure it provides useful descriptions.\r\n\r\n**Accessible Notifications**\r\n\r\n- [x] Implement ARIA live regions for dynamic elements like error messages and toasts.\r\n\r\n**Testing**\r\n\r\n- [x] Conduct usability testing with keyboard-only navigation to ensure full functionality.\r\n- [x] Validate that all elements meet WCAG AA standards for accessibility.\r\n"

  "body": "### Epic 6: Sales and Analytics\r\n\r\n*As an admin, I can view a list of the top-selling products so that I can focus on promoting high-performing items.*\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Acceptance Criteria**\r\n\r\n- Admins can view a dynamically generated list of the top-selling products.\r\n- Each product entry includes details such as product name, total units sold, and total revenue generated.\r\n- The list can be filtered by time period (e.g., last week, last month, last year).\r\n- The list is sorted by total units sold in descending order by default.\r\n- Admins can export the top-selling products list as a CSV file for external analysis.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Tasks**\r\n\r\n**Top-Selling Products List**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Create a section on the analytics dashboard to display the top-selling products.\r\n- [ ] Include metrics such as product name, total units sold, and revenue for each product.\r\n\r\n**Filtering Options**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Implement filters to allow admins to view top-selling products for specific time periods (e.g., last week, last month).\r\n- [ ] Ensure filters update the list dynamically.\r\n\r\n**Export Functionality**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Add a button to export the top-selling products list as a CSV file.\r\n- [ ] Ensure the exported CSV reflects the selected time period and contains all relevant data.\r\n\r\n**Default Sorting**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Automatically sort the list by total units sold in descending order.\r\n- [ ] Allow admins to change the sorting to revenue or other metrics if needed.\r\n\r\n**Testing**\r\n\r\n- [ ] Verify the top-selling products list is generated accurately based on sales data.\r\n- [ ] Test the filtering functionality to ensure it updates the list correctly.\r\n- [ ] Validate the CSV export functionality for completeness and accuracy.\r\n- [ ] Ensure the interface is responsive and works across multiple devices and browsers.\r\n\r\n---\r\n"
}

and visually appealing on desktop, tablet, and mobile devices.\r\n- Main navigation and footer are intuitive and accessible on all pages.\r\n- Interactive elements (buttons, links, forms) provide clear feedback and are easy to use.\r\n- Toast notifications display relevant messages for user actions, such as success, errors, or warnings.\r\n- Pages load quickly, with minimal delay even for image-heavy content.\r\n\r\n---\r\n\r\n**Tasks**\r\n\r\n**General Layout and Branding**\r\n\r\n- [x] Implement a consistent style guide for fonts, colors, and layout across all pages using the *base.css* file.\r\n- [x] Update the logo and favicon to be consistent and visible across all templates.\r\n- [x] Review and enhance the hero image and other visuals in the */static/images/* directory.\r\n\r\n**Responsive Design**\r\n\r\n- [x] Develop CSS rules for mobile responsiveness, ensuring elements adjust seamlessly across screen sizes.\r\n- [ ] Test pages like *index.html*, *product_detail.html*, and *checkout.html* on multiple devices to verify responsiveness.\r\n\r\n**Navigation and Footer**\r\n\r\n- [x] Add intuitive navigation with links to key pages in *main-nav.html*.\r\n- [x] Create a footer template linking to the *Privacy Policy* and *About Us* pages.\r\n\r\n**Accessibility**\r\n\r\n- [x] Add ARIA attributes to buttons and interactive elements to improve accessibility.\r\n- [x] Check text contrast and color schemes for WCAG compliance using tools like Lighthouse.\r\n\r\n**Toast Notifications**\r\n\r\n- [x] Enhance toast templates (e.g., *toast_success.html*, *toast_error.html*) for better feedback.\r\n- [x] Use *dynamic-messages.js* to display toast notifications dynamically.\r\n\r\n**Page Load Optimization**\r\n\r\n- [x] Compress image files in the */media/* folder for faster loading.\r\n- [x] Minify and optimize CSS and JavaScript files in */static/css/* and */static/js/*.\r\n\r\n**Testing**\r\n\r\n- [x] Conduct end-to-end testing of the design, responsiveness, navigation, and interactive features.\r\n- [x] Validate that all pages meet the acceptance criteria before release.\r\n"
